<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">го́жий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">góžij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*goditi</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">прыго́жы</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pryhóžy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folklore or poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> beautiful, good-looking</li>
<li>(of weather) clear, bright, sunny</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***придавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a> (3607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придать.html>прида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pridátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придать.html>прида́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give, to impart; to attach</li>
<li>to increase, to strengthen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смелость.html>сме́лости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pridavátʹ</b> smélosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to increase braveness</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 13b.
<i><a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>Придава́ть</a> + <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. п., <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a> + <a href = vnd.unilang:разделить.html>разде́лит</a>. п.; <a href = vnd.unilang:придавать.html>придава́ть</a> + <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́т</a>. п.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:придать.html>прида́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-да-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:придавить.html>придави́ть</a> (7974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавить.html>придави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придавливать.html>прида́вливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to press <i>(against)</i>, to press down <i>(against)</i>, to weigh down <i>(against)</i>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>giving, conferring, imparting, communication
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>pridánija</b> síly</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">(in order) to give strength</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:придание.html>прида́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:законный.html>зако́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>pridánija</b> zakónnoj síly</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">(in order) to validate; (in order) to make legally binding</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***придаток.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:придаток.html>прида́ток</a> (20743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придать.html>прида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pridátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придаток.html>прида́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pridátok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придаток.html>прида́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придаток.html>прида́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:придаток.html>прида́тков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>appendage, addition, supplement</li>
